Unless otherwise determined by the Committee, the number of Tranche I PRSUs that become earned based on the attainment of the applicable run rate performance goals will be reduced by 25% if such goals are not attained within T-Mobile&#8217;s annualized capital expenditure budget over the applicable performance period.  </span></div><div
